The press release is furnished with this filing as Exhibit 99.1.</p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:10pt; FONT-FAMILY:Times New Roman; TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:4.5pt 0pt 0pt; TEXT-JUSTIFY:inter-ideograph">&nbsp;</p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:10pt; FONT-FAMILY:Times New Roman; TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:4.5pt 0pt 0pt; TEXT-JUSTIFY:inter-ideograph">The Company also has made a presentation available to investors on the Investor Relations section of its website at www.swn.com/investors. The Company does not undertake to update the information contained in the presentation but may update the presentation from time to time and provide other announcements and presentations relating to its financial and operational performance and other matters, through its investor relations website at www.swn.com/investors, for purposes of making such information "publicly available" under Regulation FD promulgated by the Securities and Exchange Commission. Investors are urged to monitor the Company's website for announcements of material events relating to the Company.</p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:10pt; FONT-FAMILY:Times New Roman; TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:4.5pt 0pt 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN:center; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal"> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; FONT-FAMILY:Times; TEXT-ALIGN:center; MARGIN:0pt"><font style="FONT-FAMILY:Arial; FONT-WEIGHT:bold; TEXT-DECORATION:underline; DISPLAY:inline">SOUTHWESTERN ENERGY ANNOUNCES COMPANY UPDATE </font></p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; FONT-FAMILY:Times; TEXT-ALIGN:center; MARGIN:0pt"><font style="FONT-FAMILY:Arial; FONT-WEIGHT:bold; TEXT-DECORATION:underline; DISPLAY:inline">AND GUIDANCE FOR 2015</font> </p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; FONT-FAMILY:Times; TEXT-ALIGN:center; MARGIN:0pt">&nbsp;</p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; FONT-FAMILY:Times; TEXT-ALIGN:center; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal"> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; BORDER-BOTTOM:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%; TEXT-INDENT:0pt"><font style="FONT-FAMILY:Arial; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); DISPLAY:inline">Houston, Texas &#150; December 29, 2014... Southwestern Energy Company (NYSE: SWN) posted an updated presentation to its website with materials that are planned to be discussed on its company update call on December 30, 2014.&nbsp;&nbsp;Included in this material are details about the recent acquisition of southwest Marcellus and Utica assets along with the company&#146;s plans for 2015.</font> </p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; BORDER-BOTTOM:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%; TEXT-INDENT:0pt">&nbsp;</p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; BORDER-TOP:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; BORDER-BOTTOM:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%; TEXT-INDENT:0pt"> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; BORDER-TOP:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; BORDER-BOTTOM:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%; TEXT-INDENT:0pt"><font style="FONT-FAMILY:Arial; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); DISPLAY:inline">&#147;These are exciting times at Southwestern Energy,&#148; stated</font><font style="FONT-FAMILY:Arial; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); DISPLAY:inline"> Steve Mueller, Chairman and Chief Executive Officer of Southwestern Energy.&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;The addition of this third world-class asset into the portfolio allows us to add even more value for shareholders for years to come.&nbsp;&nbsp;Our total current net acreage of 782,000 acres and net production of approximately 1.2 Bcf</font><font style="FONT-FAMILY:Arial; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); DISPLAY:inline">e</font><font style="FONT-FAMILY:Arial; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); DISPLAY:inline"> per day in the northeast United States place Southwestern Energy in the top three among our peers, and we are the only company to have significant positions in both core areas.&nbsp;&nbsp;The quality of our newest acquisition is evidenced by the proved reserves of 2.5 Tcfe as of July 1, 2014, the large inventory of high-return wells and the recent industry results for wells surrounding the area.&nbsp;&nbsp;One of those wells, the Messenger 3-H, completed by Chesapeake in Wetzel County, West Virginia in October, has produced 20 million cubic feet per day for more than 30 days from a 5,889 foot lateral in the Utica shale.&#148;</font> </p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; BORDER-TOP:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; BORDER-BOTTOM:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%; TEXT-INDENT:0pt"> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; BORDER-TOP:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; BORDER-BOTTOM:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%; TEXT-INDENT:0pt">&nbsp;</p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; BORDER-TOP:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; BORDER-BOTTOM:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%; TEXT-INDENT:0pt"><font style="FONT-FAMILY:Arial; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); DISPLAY:inline">The company believes the acquired acreage is prospective in a minimum of three zones, including the Upper Devonian, the Marcellus and the Utica shales, that will ultimately total net recoverable volumes of over 45 Tcfe.&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;This world-class quality and our demonstrated operational innovation are key components combining to create long-term double-digit growth in production and returns for our shareholders.&nbsp;&nbsp;Consistently delivering industry leading returns, focused improvement and continuous innovation are exemplified by our significant growth and improving performance in the Fayetteville and Marcellus shales.&nbsp;&nbsp;This transaction adds to the already strong portfolio with another large top-tier quality project, allowing us once again to leverage our operational strengths and deliver results.&#148; </font></p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; BORDER-TOP:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; BORDER-BOTTOM:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%; TEXT-INDENT:0pt"> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; BORDER-TOP:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; BORDER-BOTTOM:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%; TEXT-INDENT:0pt">&nbsp;</p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; BORDER-TOP:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; BORDER-BOTTOM:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%; TEXT-INDENT:0pt"><font style="FONT-FAMILY:Arial; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); DISPLAY:inline">&#147;Our approach to innovation has also allowed us to capture opportunities in places off the beaten path from the rest of the industry.&nbsp;&nbsp;In addition to discovering the Fayetteville shale and the early recognition of the potential of the prolific northeast corner of Pennsylvania, we have amassed more than 1.7 million exploration acres in several plays.&nbsp;&nbsp;Early results from the first horizontal well in a recently announced project that includes more than 375,000 net acres in the Sand Wash basin in Colorado are encouraging.&nbsp;&nbsp;The Welker 6-92 1-2H in Moffat County has been testing for approximately 2 weeks and has a 7-day average production of 408 barrels of oil per day, 448 thousand cubic feet of gas and 1,193 barrels of completion water from a 4,663 foot lateral.&#148;&nbsp; </font></p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; BORDER-TOP:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; BORDER-BOTTOM:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%; TEXT-INDENT:0pt"> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%; TEXT-INDENT:0pt"><font style="FONT-FAMILY:Arial; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); DISPLAY:inline">The following table provides the current development plan for the company over the next three years.&nbsp; </font></p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; BORDER-BOTTOM:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%; TEXT-INDENT:0pt"><img src=wellcount3yearplan.jpg></p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; </font></p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; FONT-FAMILY:Cambria; FONT-WEIGHT:bold; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); MARGIN:24pt 0pt 0pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; FONT-FAMILY:Arial; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); TEXT-DECORATION:underline; DISPLAY:inline"><img src=targetrange.jpg></font></p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; FONT-FAMILY:Cambria; FONT-WEIGHT:bold; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); MARGIN:24pt 0pt 0pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; FONT-FAMILY:Arial; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); TEXT-DECORATION:underline; DISPLAY:inline">Capital Investment Plan for 2015</font> </p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; FONT-FAMILY:Cambria; FONT-WEIGHT:bold; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); MARGIN:24pt 0pt 0pt">&nbsp;</p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; BORDER-BOTTOM:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%; TEXT-INDENT:0pt"> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; BORDER-TOP:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; BORDER-BOTTOM:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%; TEXT-INDENT:0pt"><font style="FONT-FAMILY:Arial; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); DISPLAY:inline">With this expanded portfolio of opportunities, the company&#146;s total capital investment program in 2015 is planned to be approximately $2.6 billion, compared to a projected $2.4 billion capital program in 2014, excluding the acquisition capital for transactions announced in the fourth quarter of 2014.</font> </p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; BORDER-TOP:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%; TEXT-INDENT:0pt"> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; BORDER-TOP:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%; TEXT-INDENT:0pt">&nbsp;</p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; BORDER-BOTTOM:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%; TEXT-INDENT:0pt"><font style="FONT-FAMILY:Arial; DISPLAY:inline">Southwestern is targeting total net gas and oil production of 970 to 980 Bcfe in 2015, up approximately 28% over the company&#146;s current production projection of 758 to 764 Bcfe for 2014 (using midpoints). Total net production from Southwest Appalachia is expected to be 145 to 150 Bcfe, of which approximately 40% is estimated to be liquids.&nbsp;&nbsp;In Northeast Appalachia, the company expects total net production to continue its strong growth in 2015 to 345 to 350 Bcf, compared to 253 to 254 Bcf that is projected to be produced in 2014.&nbsp;&nbsp;Total net production from the Fayetteville Shale in 2015 is expected to be 470 to 475 Bcf.&nbsp;&nbsp;Both the conventional Arkoma and East Texas assets are assumed to be sold effective January 1, 2015. </font></p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; BORDER-TOP:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%; TEXT-INDENT:0pt"> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; BORDER-TOP:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%; TEXT-INDENT:0pt">&nbsp;</p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; FONT-FAMILY:Times; TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt"><font style="FONT-FAMILY:Arial; DISPLAY:inline">&#147;2015 will be a transformational year for Southwestern Energy,&#148; stated Mueller. &#147;Our Northeast Appalachia and Fayetteville assets will continue to exhibit strong performance and demonstrate their ability to generate significant returns.&nbsp;&nbsp;At the same time, the company will hit the ground running in Southwest Appalachia with substantial activities planned and strong results expected while accelerating up the learning curve.&nbsp;&nbsp;With the quality of our three world-class assets, the strength of our firm transportation portfolio and our operational experience and focus, 2015 is setting up to be a very exciting and transformational year for Southwestern Energy.&#148;</font> </p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; FONT-FAMILY:Times; TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal"> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; FONT-FAMILY:Times; TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt"> <p> <hr width=100% size=3 style=COLOR:rgb(153,153,153) align=center> <p style=PAGE-BREAK-AFTER:always>&nbsp;</p> <div style=WIDTH:100%> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; FONT-FAMILY:Times; MARGIN:0pt"> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; FONT-FAMILY:Times; MARGIN:0pt" /></div> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; FONT-FAMILY:Times; TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt"><font style="FONT-FAMILY:Arial; DISPLAY:inline">The following tables provide annual forecast information for 2015, as compared to projected 2014 results, for capital</font><font style="FONT-FAMILY:Arial; FONT-WEIGHT:bold; DISPLAY:inline">&nbsp;</font><font style="FONT-FAMILY:Arial; DISPLAY:inline">investments and the gross and net well counts for each of the company&#146;s operating areas.</font> </p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; FONT-FAMILY:Times; TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt">&nbsp;</p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; FONT-FAMILY:Times; TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal"> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; BORDER-BOTTOM:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%; TEXT-INDENT:0pt">&nbsp;<img width=722 height=407 style="HEIGHT:349px; WIDTH:674px" src=capitalinvestmentstable.jpg></p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; BORDER-BOTTOM:0px; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%; TEXT-INDENT:0pt">&nbsp;</p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; BORDER-TOP:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; BORDER-BOTTOM:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%; TEXT-INDENT:0pt">&nbsp;<img width=913 height=280 style="HEIGHT:234px; WIDTH:710px" src=wellcounttable.jpg>&nbsp;</p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; BORDER-TOP:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; BORDER-BOTTOM:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%; TEXT-INDENT:0pt"><strong></strong>&nbsp;</p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; BORDER-TOP:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; BORDER-BOTTOM:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%; TEXT-INDENT:0pt">&nbsp;</p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; BORDER-TOP:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; BORDER-BOTTOM:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%; TEXT-INDENT:0pt">&nbsp;</p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; BORDER-TOP:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; BORDER-BOTTOM:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%; TEXT-INDENT:0pt"><font style="FONT-FAMILY:Arial; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); DISPLAY:inline">In Southwest Appalachia, the company currently has a total of 443,000 net acres with net production of approximately 370 MMcfe per day from approximately 1,500 wells.&nbsp;&nbsp;More than 95% of the production is from approximately 256 horizontal wells completed in the Marcellus and the Utica intervals.&nbsp;&nbsp;Reserves as of mid-year 2014 are 2.5 Tcfe and more than 5,300 wells will be needed to recover the 45 Tcfe net potential for Southwestern Energy.&nbsp;&nbsp;The company plans to begin 2015 running one rig and increase throughout the year to end the year at four rigs.&nbsp;&nbsp;The company expects that the </font><font style="FONT-FAMILY:Arial; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); DISPLAY:inline">average re-entry to re-entry</font><font style="FONT-FAMILY:Arial; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); DISPLAY:inline">&nbsp;</font><font style="FONT-FAMILY:Arial; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); DISPLAY:inline">time to drill its operated horizontal wells to total depth </font><font style="FONT-FAMILY:Arial; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); DISPLAY:inline">will be approximately 20 days and, assuming a horizontal lateral length of 7,500 feet, the average completed well cost to be approximately $9 million. </font></p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; BORDER-TOP:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; BORDER-BOTTOM:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%; TEXT-INDENT:0pt">&nbsp;</p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; BORDER-TOP:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; BORDER-BOTTOM:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%; TEXT-INDENT:0pt"> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; BORDER-TOP:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; BORDER-BOTTOM:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%; TEXT-INDENT:0pt"><font style="FONT-FAMILY:Arial; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); DISPLAY:inline">Earlier this month, Southwestern announced the acquisition of 46,700 net acres and an additional 260 million cubic feet per day of firm transport in northeast Pennsylvania.&nbsp;&nbsp;This acreage includes more than 200 Bcfe of proved reserves that will be booked at the time of closing in the first quarter of 2015 and has significant upside as indicated by two nearby well tests in Susquehanna County by Southwestern in the third quarter.&nbsp; </font><font style="FONT-FAMILY:Arial; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); DISPLAY:inline">The Hughes North 1H has completed the entire lateral length of 4,981 feet and had a maximum 24-hour rate of 4.7 million cubic feet per day. The Dayton 4H has a total lateral length of 5,278 feet and tested a maximum 24-hour rate of 4.5 million cubic feet </font></p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; BORDER-TOP:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; BORDER-BOTTOM:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%; TEXT-INDENT:0pt">&nbsp;</p> <p> <hr width=100% size=3 style=COLOR:rgb(153,153,153) align=center> <p style=PAGE-BREAK-AFTER:always>&nbsp;</p> <div style=WIDTH:100%> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; FONT-FAMILY:Times; MARGIN:0pt"> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; FONT-FAMILY:Times; MARGIN:0pt" /></div> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; BORDER-TOP:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; BORDER-BOTTOM:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%"><font style="FONT-FAMILY:Arial; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); DISPLAY:inline">per day from the first 30% that is completed to date.&nbsp; </font><font style="FONT-FAMILY:Arial; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); DISPLAY:inline">In 2015, Southwestern plans to drill approximately 80 wells in Susquehanna County, 14 wells in Bradford County, 4 wells in Lycoming County and 7 horizontal delineation wells on the company&#146;s acreage in Wyoming, Sullivan and Tioga Counties. Included in the 2015 drilling activity are 4 wells that will target the Upper Marcellus.&nbsp;&nbsp;The company expects that the </font><font style="FONT-FAMILY:Arial; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); DISPLAY:inline">average re-entry to re-entry</font><font style="FONT-FAMILY:Arial; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); DISPLAY:inline">&nbsp;</font><font style="FONT-FAMILY:Arial; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); DISPLAY:inline">time to drill its operated horizontal wells to total depth </font><font style="FONT-FAMILY:Arial; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); DISPLAY:inline">will be approximately 10.1 days in 2015, compared to approximately 10.3 days projected for 2014. Southwestern&#146;s average 2015 completed well cost is estimated to be $6.8 million per well with a 5,520 average horizontal lateral with 14.0 completed stages, compared to an estimated $6.4 million well cost with an average horizontal lateral length of 4,566 feet and 15.4 completed stages in 2014. </font></p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; BORDER-TOP:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; BORDER-BOTTOM:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%">&nbsp;</p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; BORDER-TOP:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; BORDER-BOTTOM:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%; TEXT-INDENT:0pt"> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; BORDER-TOP:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%; TEXT-INDENT:0pt"><font style="FONT-FAMILY:Arial; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); DISPLAY:inline">Recent well results in the Fayetteville shale continue to improve.&nbsp;&nbsp;Initial production from wells completed in October and November are on a record pace of averaging nearly 5 MMcf per day.&nbsp;&nbsp;The previous quarterly record was 4.9 MMcf per day in the fourth quarter of 2013. In 2015, Southwestern expects that the </font><font style="FONT-FAMILY:Arial; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); DISPLAY:inline">average re-entry to re-entry</font><font style="FONT-FAMILY:Arial; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); DISPLAY:inline">&nbsp;</font><font style="FONT-FAMILY:Arial; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); DISPLAY:inline">time to drill its operated horizontal wells to total depth </font><font style="FONT-FAMILY:Arial; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); DISPLAY:inline">will decrease in 2015 to approximately 6.3 days from approximately 6.8 days projected for 2014 as a result of efficiencies associated with the new rig fleet. The company&#146;s average 2015 completed well cost is estimated to be $2.6 million per well with a 5,075 average horizontal lateral, compared to an estimated $2.6 million well cost with an average horizontal lateral length of 5,000 feet in 2014.&nbsp;&nbsp;Additionally, Southwestern continues to drill the Upper Fayetteville formation and a total of 46 wells have been drilled to date.&nbsp;&nbsp;The company expects to drill approximately 20 Upper Fayetteville wells in 2015. </font></p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; BORDER-TOP:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%; TEXT-INDENT:0pt">&nbsp;</p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; FONT-FAMILY:Times; TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal"> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; BORDER-BOTTOM:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%; TEXT-INDENT:0pt"><font style="FONT-FAMILY:Arial; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); DISPLAY:inline">In the Sand Wash Basin, the company expects to drill an additional 5 wells in 2015 as progress continues in testing the acreage acquired in 2014.&nbsp;&nbsp;To date, the company has drilled 5 wells and, as previously mentioned, is encouraged by the initial results.&nbsp; </font></p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; BORDER-TOP:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; BORDER-BOTTOM:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%; TEXT-INDENT:0pt"> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; BORDER-TOP:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; BORDER-BOTTOM:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%; TEXT-INDENT:0pt">&nbsp;</p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; BORDER-TOP:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; BORDER-BOTTOM:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%; TEXT-INDENT:0pt"><font style="FONT-FAMILY:Arial; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); DISPLAY:inline">In the company&#146;s Brown Dense exploration program, Southwestern is interpreting the 75 miles of 3-D seismic that was obtained in late 2014 and is planning to drill at least two wells in 2015.&nbsp; </font></p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; BORDER-TOP:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; BORDER-BOTTOM:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%; TEXT-INDENT:0pt">&nbsp;</p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; BORDER-TOP:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; BORDER-BOTTOM:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%; TEXT-INDENT:0pt"> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; BORDER-TOP:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; BORDER-BOTTOM:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%; TEXT-INDENT:0pt"> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; BORDER-TOP:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%; TEXT-INDENT:0pt"><font style="FONT-FAMILY:Arial; FONT-WEIGHT:bold; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); TEXT-DECORATION:underline; DISPLAY:inline">Southwestern Issues Guidance for 2015</font> </p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; BORDER-TOP:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); TEXT-ALIGN:justify; see Explanation and Reconciliation of Non-GAAP Financial Measures below.</font></p></td></tr></table></div> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; FONT-FAMILY:Times; TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal"> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; FONT-FAMILY:Times; TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal">&nbsp;</p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%; TEXT-INDENT:0pt"><font style="FONT-FAMILY:Arial; FONT-WEIGHT:bold; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); TEXT-DECORATION:underline; DISPLAY:inline">Explanation and Reconciliation of Non-GAAP Financial Measures</font> </p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%; TEXT-INDENT:0pt">&nbsp;</p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; FONT-FAMILY:Times New Roman; TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt"> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; BORDER-BOTTOM:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%; TEXT-INDENT:0pt"><font style="FONT-FAMILY:Arial; COLOR:rgb(0,0,0); DISPLAY:inline">Net cash provided by operating activities before changes in operating assets and liabilities (net cash flow) is presented because of its acceptance as an indicator of an oil and gas exploration and production company&#146;s ability to internally fund exploration and development activities and to service or incur additional debt. The company has also included this information because changes in operating assets and liabilities relate to the timing of cash receipts and disbursements which the company may not control and may not relate to the period in which the operating activities occurred. Net cash provided by operating activities before changes in operating assets and liabilities should not be considered in isolation or as a substitute for net cash provided by operating activities prepared in accordance with generally accepted accounting </font></p> <p> <hr width=100% size=3 style=COLOR:rgb(153,153,153) align=center> <p style=PAGE-BREAK-AFTER:always>&nbsp;</p> <div style=WIDTH:100%> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; FONT-FAMILY:Times; MARGIN:0pt"> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; FONT-FAMILY:Times; MARGIN:0pt" /></div> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; BORDER-BOTTOM:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%"><font style="FONT-FAMILY:Arial; DISPLAY:inline">principles. The table below reconciles 2015 forecasted net cash provided by operating activities before changes in operating assets and liabilities with 2015 forecasted net cash provided by operating activities. </font></p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; BORDER-BOTTOM:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%">&nbsp;</p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; BORDER-TOP:rgb(217,217,217) 1pt; FONT-FAMILY:CG Times; TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:100%; TEXT-INDENT:0pt"> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; FONT-FAMILY:Times; TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt"><img src=f2015guidancecashflow.jpg>&nbsp;</p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; FONT-FAMILY:Times; TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal"> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; FONT-FAMILY:Times; TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt"><font style="FONT-FAMILY:Arial; DISPLAY:inline">EBITDA is defined as net income plus interest expense, income tax expense, depreciation, depletion and amortization. Southwestern has included information concerning EBITDA because it is used by certain investors as a measure of the ability of a company to service or incur indebtedness and because it is a financial measure commonly used in the energy industry. EBITDA should not be considered in isolation or as a substitute for net income, net cash provided by operating activities or other income or cash flow data prepared in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles or as a measure of the company's profitability or liquidity. EBITDA as defined above may not be comparable to similarly titled measures of other companies. Net income is a financial measure calculated and presented in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles. The table below reconciles 2015 forecasted EBITDA with 2015 forecasted net income. </font></p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; FONT-FAMILY:Times; TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt">&nbsp;</p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; FONT-FAMILY:Times; TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal"> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; FONT-FAMILY:Times; TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt"><img width=955 height=365 style="HEIGHT:291px; WIDTH:802px" src=f2015guidanceebitda.jpg>&nbsp;</p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; FONT-FAMILY:Times; TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt; LINE-HEIGHT:normal"> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; FONT-FAMILY:Times; TEXT-ALIGN:justify; MARGIN:0pt"><font style="FONT-FAMILY:Arial; DISPLAY:inline">Southwestern Energy Company is an independent energy company whose wholly-owned subsidiaries are engaged in natural gas and oil exploration, development and production, natural gas gathering and marketing. Additional information on the company can be found on the Internet at </font><font style="FONT-FAMILY:Arial; TEXT-DECORATION:underline; DISPLAY:inline">http://www.swn.com</font><font style="FONT-FAMILY:Arial; DISPLAY:inline">.</font> </p> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt; FONT-FAMILY:Times; MARGIN:0pt"> <p> <hr width=100% size=3 style=COLOR:rgb(153,153,153) align=center> <p style=PAGE-BREAK-AFTER:always>&nbsp;</p> <div style=WIDTH:100%> <p style="FONT-SIZE:12pt;
